posted:Posted July 14, 2023
msg:In the hot summer season, I brought my parents in their 80s to the Garden Expo. The essence is to find a place with a good view to spend two days in a hotel, so the hotel's location and service quality are particularly important. I did a lot of homework beforehand, read a lot of Ctrip reviews and Xiaohongshu strategy, and finally chose Radisson. Let me talk about the conclusion first: the right choice makes the journey perfect!

1. Geographic location. Just next to "Su Yunhui Valley", the balcony of the garden-view twin room we booked can see the "Jingyang Tower" of Nanjing Garden. The weather is too hot to go out during the day, so I went to the nearby gardens at 7:00 in the morning, and then went back to the hotel for breakfast, which was very convenient. Parents are very satisfied with living in this location!

2. Catering. It is a few minutes' walk from the "Yechun" tea house in Yangzhou Garden. The three-person set meal on Dianping is full of portions and delicious, and my parents like it very much. The dishes in the hotel's Chinese restaurant "Suxiu" are good, but the prices are slightly higher.

3. The swimming pool. The scenery is beautiful and the water is clean. However, there are only four deck chairs in the entire swimming pool. If there are too many people, it will not be possible to take turns. It is recommended that the open shower area next to it be changed into a rest area.

4. Service. This is what I think is the biggest factor that separates the five-star hotels. After all, everyone is looking for a good mood when they go on vacation, and service is the most important thing.

(1) Front desk: I called the front desk of the hotel before checking in. The young lady had a very good attitude and patiently listened to my needs, saying that she would try her best to arrange according to the room situation of the day. When checking in, the little brother named Jiang at the front desk had a very good attitude and said that he had arranged a room for us in advance. Great first experience! Appreciate and thank you for the service at the front desk!

(2) Catering: The dinner service in the Chinese restaurant is very good. The lady speaks softly and is attentive. The whole dining process is very comfortable. But the breakfast service hopes to be improved. The service of the entire western restaurant, from the manager on duty to the waiter, is full of cold temperament. Even the most polite words make people feel insincere. I hope to learn more about the service with a smile. Remind that when the meal time is approaching, the tall guy is very close to me, tall and expressionless, I need to look up to God to see him.

(3) Swimming pool: There are no lifeguards in the swimming pool, only waiters wearing leather shoes and playing with mobile phones. The tall male waiter in the afternoon of the first day was not bad. He often paid attention to the dynamics of the swimming pool, responded to guests in a timely manner, and took the initiative to fetch mineral water. The next afternoon, the short male waiter kept playing with his mobile phone without raising his head, nor did he bring water to the guests. I went to the cupboard to get water for my dad who came ashore after swimming, but he still didn‚Äôt raise his head. Don't look up!

(4) Shuttle bus: All the shuttle bus drivers I met were very nice and polite, and they were very patient in answering inquiries, because the various route settings in the Garden Expo Park were really a bit messy. Then I called the hotel twice, and both quickly provided solutions, once to show us where to buy tickets for the small train, and once to send a shuttle bus to pick us up back to the hotel. Therefore, if there is a problem in the park, calling the hotel will solve the problem efficiently and give you a sense of security.

In general, the flaws do not conceal the virtues. Thanks for the hospitality, there will be a period later.

The architectural style of the lobby is full of holiday a**osphere, and the concierge and front desk are courteous, making people feel like a spring breeze as soon as they enter the hotel.
Guest room: Because the tenth anniversary of the marriage was noted when booking, the hotel upgraded the executive room, which is full of sincerity. Entering the room, the big bed has been arranged, which is very pleasant! Although there is no private soup in the room, the oversized round bathtub üõÅ is also very comfortable to soak in, and you can also soak while watching TV. The whole house intelligent system in the room, no need to insert the room card, the door is automatically activated, and the degree of intelligence is high.
Hotel facilities: There are very few people staying in the outdoor pool on Friday. It is a special feeling to introduce Tangshan hot spring water to soak in the soup under the starry sky and bright moon; the swimming pool is a classic Internet celebrity check-in place, with 270 window views, you can swim while enjoying the view; the service of the executive lounge is special Good, kind and pleasant, just right, meticulous, compared to the general executive lounge with more desserts and sweets, it is uniquely equipped with Chinese dishes.
Service: The service staff who come into contact with the hotel take the initiative to say hello and provide service with a smile. Because it was the tenth anniversary of the wedding, Li Yan, the manager of the executive floor of the hotel, gave her blessings on the phone before checking in. After checking in, she even sent gifts üéÅ and hand-painted greeting cards in person, which is enough to show that she is full of heart ‚ù§Ô∏è and will choose it again. Check in again.
